[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mReport[0m===                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         A fuzzing run triggered a critical security exception indicating a file path        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         traversal vulnerability in the Apache POI POIFSDump utility. The Jazzer sanitizer   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         detected that a crafted input caused the code to attempt accessing a path outside   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         the intended directory hierarchy [1m([0m`..[35m/../../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m`[1m)[0m. The exception    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         surfaced in the file path sanitizer before any further processing of the malicious  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         input.                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Issue manifestation                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           A libFuzzer-generated test case caused the following exception during execution   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         of `POIPOIFSDumpFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`:                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           ```                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         traversal: [35m/tmp/expander-.../[0m[95mRoot[0m Entry/..[35m/../../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             at                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcom.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal.check[0m[1m([0mFilePathTraversal.j [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         av[1;92ma:346[0m[1m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             at                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcom.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal.checkPath[0m[1m([0mFilePathTravers [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         al.jav[1;92ma:293[0m[1m)[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             at                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcom.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal.pathFirstArgHook[0m[1m([0mFilePath [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Traversal.jav[1;92ma:177[0m[1m)[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             at [1;35morg.apache.poi.poifs.dev.POIFSDump.dump[0m[1m([0mPOIFSDump.jav[1;92ma:108[0m[1m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             at [1;35morg.apache.poi.poifs.dev.POIFSDump.main[0m[1m([0mPOIFSDump.jav[1;92ma:80[0m[1m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             at                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35morg.apache.poi.POIPOIFSDumpFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1m([0mPOIPOIFSDumpFuzzer.jav[1;92ma:74[0m[1m)[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           ```                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Vulnerability type                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           The issue is identified as a file path traversal vulnerability. The fuzzer’s      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         security sanitizer halted execution when it detected an attempt to navigate outside [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         of the intended directory via “..” segments in the input path.                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Important observations                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The exception originates in Jazzer’s `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer, which hooks [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         into file-access APIs and flags disallowed path patterns.                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The offending call chain leads from `POIPOIFSDumpFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0mthe harness[1m)[0m into `POIFSDump.dump` and `POIFSDump.main`, where file paths derived  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         from parsed POIFS [1m([0mOLE2[1m)[0m entries are passed unchecked to file I/O routines.         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The harness merely invokes the target code with fuzzer-supplied byte arrays; it [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         is not the root cause of path traversal but provides the entry point that exercises [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         it.                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The crash input is a libFuzzer-generated binary blob designed to exercise edge  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         cases in POI’s POIFS handling, ultimately producing a malicious path string.        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Code areas for investigation                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           To fully understand the issue and its context, the following parts of the         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         codebase should be reviewed:                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m1[0m. `org.apache.poi.poifs.dev.POIFSDump.dump` [1m([0maround line [1;36m108[0m[1m)[0m – how entry names  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         are read and converted into file system paths.                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m2[0m. `org.apache.poi.poifs.dev.POIFSDump.main` [1m([0maround line [1;36m80[0m[1m)[0m – argument parsing  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         and dispatch to `dump`.                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m3[0m. Any file-writing or file-reading utilities in the POIFS developer tools that   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         translate POIFS entry names into on-disk file paths.                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m4[0m. The fuzzer harness `POIPOIFSDumpFuzzer` to confirm which API calls are being   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         exercised and how input bytes are mapped to POIFS entry names.                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m5[0m. Interaction points between POI path-handling code and Jazzer’s                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer to identify the exact path concatenation or           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         normalization steps that lead to traversal sequences.                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         No assumptions are made about the underlying cause beyond the observed path         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         traversal, and no remediation steps are proposed here, per instructions.            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Initial Issue Log                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The codebase’s POIFSDump utility is subject to a file path traversal issue, as      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         identified by Jazzer’s `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical`. The initial crash log shows   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         that malicious entry names containing “..” segments allow writes outside the        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         intended output directory. A patch was applied that replaces the raw entry name     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         with its last path segment [1m([0m`[1;35mPaths.get[0m[1m([0mname[1m)[0m[1;35m.getFileName[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1;35m.toString[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`[1m)[0m, intending  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         to strip any directory traversal components. However, after applying this patch,    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         the same Jazzer exception is still triggered in `POIFSDump.dump`, indicating the    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         traversal check continues to flag a violation.                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Initial Issue                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - A Jazzer fuzzing run crashes with `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         traversal`.                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The exception stack traces into `FilePathTraversal.check` and ultimately into     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `POIFSDump.dump`.                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The reported file path includes “Root Entry/..[35m/../../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m”,        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         demonstrating the use of “..” segments to escape the intended output directory.     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Patch Attempt                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Added an import for `java.nio.file.Path`.                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - In `[1;35mPOIFSDump.dump[0m[1m([0mPOIFSFileSystem fs, int startBlock, String name, File          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         parent[1m)[0m`:                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • Compute `safeName` as the file name segment only:                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             `String safeName = [1;35mPaths.get[0m[1m([0mname[1m)[0m[1;35m.getFileName[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1;35m.toString[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m;`                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • Construct `File file = new [1;35mFile[0m[1m([0mparent, safeName[1m)[0m;` instead of using the raw    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `name`.                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • Preserve directory creation logic and output stream opening around              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mfile.toPath[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`.                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Resulting Behavior                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - After recompilation and rerunning the fuzzer, the same                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path traversal` exception is reported at         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `POIFSDump.dump` [1m([0mline [1;36m109[0m in the patched version[1m)[0m.                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The path in the exception log still reflects traversal attempts [1m([0me.g., “Root      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Entry/..[35m/../../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m”[1m)[0m, suggesting the patch did not prevent the      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         vulnerability from being detected by the sanitizer.                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
